# ----------------------- Biological Ascensions ---------------------------
 # --------------- T1
	situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1 = {
		# Note: uses event range tec_ascension_biological.10XX
		desc = {
			text = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_desc
			trigger = {
				hidden_trigger = {
					owner = {
						is_gestalt = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		desc = {
			text = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_desc_hivemind
			trigger = {
				hidden_trigger = {
					owner = {
						is_hive_empire = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_genetic_modification
		category = positive
		complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
		complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
		fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
		fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
		start_value = 0
		progress_direction = monodirectional

		on_monthly = {
			random_events = {
				# Nothing
				200 = 0
				# Positive random outcomes
				#1 = a
				#1 = a
				#1 = a
				# Negative random outcomes
				#1 = a
				#1 = a
				#1 = a
				# TO DO
			}
		}

		on_start = {
			set_situation_locked = yes
		}

		on_fail = {
			# This should never happen
			custom_tooltip = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_fail_tooltip
			destroy_situation = this
		}
		
		on_progress_complete = {
			# This should never happen
			custom_tooltip = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_end_tooltip
			destroy_situation = this
		}

		stages = {
			situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_stage_0 = { # Base
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_tec_0
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_orange
				#0 - 10%
				end = 10
			}
			situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_stage_1 = { # First introduction
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_1
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_yellow
				#10 - 20%
				end = 20
				on_first_enter = {
					hidden_effect = {
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_ascension.1010
						}
					}
				}
			}
			situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_stage_2 = { # Bifurcation
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_2
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_green
				#20 - 30%
				end = 30
				on_first_enter = {
					hidden_effect = {
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_ascension.1020
						}
					}
				}
			}
			situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_stage_3 = {
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_tec_unknown
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_yellow
				#30 - 100%
				end = 100
				on_first_enter = {
					hidden_effect = {
						situation_event = {
							id = tec_ascension.1030
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Approaches
			approach = { # Basic
				name = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_basic
				icon = GFX_situation_approach_research
				icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_yellow
				on_select = {
					custom_tooltip = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_tooltip
				}
				allow = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						always = yes
					}
				}
				resources = {
					category = situations
					upkeep = {
						society_research = @tec_situation_cost_low
						#mult = owner.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
			}
			approach = { # Fast
				name = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_fast
				icon = GFX_situation_approach_research
				icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_red
				on_select = {
					custom_tooltip = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_fast_tooltip
				}
				allow = {
					hidden_trigger = {
						always = yes
					}
				}
				resources = {
					category = situations
					upkeep = {
						#trigger = {
						#	owner = {
						#		has_monthly_income = {
						#			resource = society_research
						#			value >= @tec_situation_cost_low
						#		}
						#	}
						#}
						society_research = @tec_situation_cost_low
						#mult = owner.trigger:num_pops
					}
				}
			}
		# /

		monthly_progress = {
			base = 0
			# Debug
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					desc = EXCELLENT
					OR = {
						has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 5
					desc = EXCELLENT
					OR = {
						has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug_2
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug_2
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -10
					desc = EXCELLENT
					OR = {
						has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug_negative
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug_negative
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -5
					desc = EXCELLENT
					OR = {
						has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug_negative_2
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug_negative_2
						}
					}
				}
			# /
			# Approaches
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				desc = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_basic
				current_situation_approach = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_basic
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				desc = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_fast
				current_situation_approach = situation_tec_ascension_biological_neutral_t1_approach_fast
			}
			modifier = {
				mult = 0.5
				desc = tec_situation_lacking_tech
				owner = {
					tec_has_genetic_ascension_t1_techs = no
				}
			}
		}

		abort_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				exists = owner
			}
		}
	}

	on_progress_complete = {

# --------------- Gating A
situation_tec_gene_path_gate = {
	desc = {
		text = situation_tec_gene_path_gate_desc
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_society_research
	category = positive
	complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
	complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
	fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
	fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
	start_value = 0
	progress_direction = monodirectional

	on_start = {
		set_situation_locked = yes
	}

	on_fail = {
		# This should never happen, but if it does...
		owner = {
			start_situation = {
				type = situation_tec_gene_path_gate
				target = capital_scope
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = new_situation
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:new_situation = {
			set_situation_locked = no
		}
	}

	on_monthly = {
		random_events = {
			# Nothing
			200 = 0
			# Negative random outcomes
			2 = tec_gene_path.1511
			2 = tec_gene_path.1512
			#1 = tec_gene_path.1513
			# Positive random outcomes
			2 = tec_gene_path.1521
			2 = tec_gene_path.1522
			1 = tec_gene_path.1523
		}
	}
	
	on_progress_complete = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_gene_path_gate_slow
				}
				owner = {
					set_timed_country_flag = {
						flag = tec_gene_good_temp
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_gene_path_gate_fast
				}
				owner = {
					set_timed_country_flag = {
						flag = tec_gene_bad_temp
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = tec_gene_path.205
				}
			}
			destroy_situation = this
		}
		custom_tooltip = situation_tec_gene_path_gate_end_tooltip
		destroy_situation = this
	}

	stages = {
		situation_tec_gene_path_gate_stage_1 = { #25% - After unlocks approaches
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_1
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_orange
			end = 25
		}

		situation_tec_gene_path_gate_stage_2 = { #50%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_2

situation_tec_gene_path_t2 = {
	desc = {
		text = situation_tec_gene_path_t2_desc
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_society_research
	category = positive
	complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
	complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
	fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
	fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
	start_value = 0
	progress_direction = monodirectional

	on_start = {
		set_situation_locked = yes
	}

	on_fail = {
		# This should never happen, but if it does...
		owner = {
			start_situation = {
				type = situation_tec_gene_path_t2
				target = capital_scope
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = new_situation
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:new_situation = {
			set_situation_locked = no
		}
	}

	on_monthly = {
		random_events = {
			# Nothing
			200 = 0
			## Negative random outcomes
			#2 = tec_gene_path.30011
			#2 = tec_gene_path.30012
			##5 = tec_gene_path.2013
			## Positive random outcomes
			#2 = tec_gene_path.30021
			#2 = tec_gene_path.30022
			#1 = tec_gene_path.30023
		}
	}
	
	on_progress_complete = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = tec_gene_path.305
				}
			}
			destroy_situation = this
		}
		custom_tooltip = situation_tec_gene_path_t2_end_tooltip
		destroy_situation = this
	}

	stages = {
		situation_tec_gene_path_t2_stage_1 = { #25% - After unlocks approaches

						id = tec_gene_path.30025
					}
				}
			}
		}

		situation_tec_gene_path_t2_stage_3 = { #75%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_3
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_green
			end = 75
			on_first_enter = {
				hidden_effect = {
					situation_event = {
						id = tec_gene_path.30050
					}
				}
			}
		}

		situation_tec_gene_path_t2_stage_4 = { #100%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_4
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_blue
			end = 100
			on_first_enter = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_situation_flag = situation_tec_gene_path_t2_end
					#situation_event = {
					#	id = tec_gene_path.30075
					#}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Approaches
		approach = { # Slow but good
			name = situation_approach_tec_gene_path_t2_slow

			}

situation_tec_synth_path_t1 = {
	desc = {
		text = situation_tec_synth_path_t1_desc
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_tec_synthetic_first
	category = positive
	complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
	complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
	fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
	fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
	start_value = 0
	progress_direction = monodirectional

	on_start = {
		set_situation_locked = yes
	}

	on_fail = {
		# This should never happen, but if it does...
		owner = {
			start_situation = {
				type = situation_tec_synth_path_t1
				target = capital_scope
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = new_situation
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:new_situation = {
			set_situation_locked = no
		}
	}

	on_monthly = {
		random_events = {
			# Nothing
			200 = 0
			# Negative random outcomes
			2 = tec_synth_path.10011
			2 = tec_synth_path.10012
			#5 = tec_synth_path.10013
			# Positive random outcomes
			2 = tec_synth_path.10021
			2 = tec_synth_path.10022
			#1 = tec_synth_path.10023
		}
	}
	
	on_progress_complete = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = tec_synth_path.105
				}
			}
			destroy_situation = this
		}
		custom_tooltip = situation_tec_synth_path_t1_finish_tooltip
		destroy_situation = this
	}

	stages = {
		situation_tec_synth_path_t1_stage_1 = { #10% - After unlocks approaches

			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_red

				exists = owner

			owner = {

				has_technology = tech_synthetic_leaders
			}
		}
		modifier = {	# Forced volunteers
			add = 0.5

			owner = {
				has_country_flag = tec_synth_forced_subject
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_leaders
			}
		}
		modifier = {	# No theseus
			add = 0.5
			desc = situation_string_tec_synth_path_t1_no_theseus
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = tec_synth_fast_transition
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_workers
				has_technology = tech_synthetic_leaders
			}
		}
	}

	abort_trigger = {
		NOT = { exists = owner }
	}

# --------------- Gating A
situation_tec_psionic_path_gate = {
	desc = {
		text = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_desc
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_society_research
	category = positive
	complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
	complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
	fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
	fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
	start_value = 0
	progress_direction = monodirectional

	on_start = {
		set_situation_locked = yes
	}

	on_fail = {
		# This should never happen, but if it does...
		owner = {
			start_situation = {
				type = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate
				target = capital_scope
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = new_situation
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:new_situation = {
			set_situation_locked = no
		}
	}

	on_monthly = {
		random_events = {
			# Nothing
			200 = 0
			## Negative random outcomes
			#2 = tec_psionic_path.20011
			#2 = tec_psionic_path.20012
			##1 = tec_psionic_path.20013
			## Positive random outcomes
			#2 = tec_psionic_path.20021
			#2 = tec_psionic_path.20022
			##1 = tec_psionic_path.20023
		}
	}
	
	on_progress_complete = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_slow
				}
				owner = {
					set_timed_country_flag = {
						flag = tec_psi_good_temp
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_fast
				}
				owner = {
					set_timed_country_flag = {
						flag = tec_psi_bad_temp
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				country_event = {
					id = tec_psionic_path.205
				}
			}
			destroy_situation = this
		}
		custom_tooltip = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_end_tooltip
		destroy_situation = this
	}

	stages = {
		situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_stage_1 = { #25% - After unlocks approaches
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_1
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_orange
			end = 25
		}

		situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_stage_2 = { #50%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_2
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_yellow
			end = 50
			on_first_enter = {
				hidden_effect = {
					situation_event = {
						id = tec_psionic_path.20025
					}
				}
			}
		}

		situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_stage_3 = { #75%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_3
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_green
			end = 75
			on_first_enter = {
				hidden_effect = {
					situation_event = {
						id = tec_psionic_path.20050
					}
				}
			}
		}

		situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_stage_4 = { #100%
			icon = GFX_situation_stage_4
			icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_blue
			end = 100
			on_first_enter = {
				hidden_effect = {
					situation_event = {
						id = tec_psionic_path.20075
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Approaches
		approach = { # Basic
			name = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_neutral
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_research
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_yellow
			potential = {
				NOT = {
					has_situation_flag = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_unlock_approachs
				}
			}
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_neutral_tooltip
			}
			resources = {
				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = @tec_situation_cost_low
					#mult = owner.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
		}
		approach = { # Slow but good
			name = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_slow
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_genetics
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_green
			potential = {
				has_situation_flag = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_unlock_approachs
			}
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_slow_tooltip
			}
			resources = {
				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = @tec_situation_cost_low
				}
			}
		}
		approach = { # Fast but bad
			name = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_fast
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_genecrank
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_red
			potential = {
				has_situation_flag = situation_tec_psionic_path_gate_unlock_approachs
			}
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_fast_tooltip
			}
			resources = {
				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = @tec_situation_cost_high
				}
			}
		}
	# /

	monthly_progress = {
		base = 0
		# Debug
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			desc = EXCELLENT
			OR = {
				has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug
				}
			}
		}
		# Passive
		
		# Approaches
		modifier = {
			add = 1
			desc = situation_string_tec_psionic_path_gate_neutral
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_neutral
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			desc = situation_string_tec_psionic_path_gate_fast
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_fast
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 1
			desc = situation_string_tec_psionic_path_gate_slow
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_psionic_path_gate_slow
		}
	}

	abort_trigger = {
		NOT = { exists = owner }
	}
}

				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = @tec_path_cost_hybrid
					engineering_research = @tec_path_cost_hybrid
					#mult = owner.trigger:num_pops
				}
			}
		}
		approach = { # fast
			name = situation_approach_tec_replicant_path_t2_fast
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_ai
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_red
			potential = {
				exists = owner
				owner = {
					has_technology = tech_neuro_quantum_links
					has_technology = tech_gene_tailoring
				}
				has_situation_flag = situation_tec_replicant_path_t2_unlock_approachs
			}
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_replicant_path_t2_fast_tooltip
			}
			resources = {
				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = @tec_path_cost_hybrid_high
					engineering_research = @tec_path_cost_hybrid_high
				}
			}
		}
	# /

	monthly_progress = {
		base = 0
		# Debug
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				desc = EXCELLENT
				OR = {
					has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				desc = EXCELLENT
				OR = {
					has_situation_flag = situation_tec_debug_2
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = situation_tec_debug_2
					}
				}
			}
		# Passive
		
		# Approaches
		modifier = {
			add = 1
			desc = situation_string_tec_replicant_path_t2_neutral
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_replicant_path_t2_neutral
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 1
			desc = situation_string_tec_replicant_path_t2_slow
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_replicant_path_t2_slow
		}
		modifier = {
			add = 2
			desc = situation_string_tec_replicant_path_t2_fast
			current_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_replicant_path_t2_fast
		}
		modifier = {
			mult = 0.5
			desc = situation_string_tec_replicant_path_t2_slow_progress
			has_situation_flag = situation_tec_replicant_path_t2_slow_progress
		}
	}

	abort_trigger = {
		NOT = { exists = owner }
	}

situation_tec_biopsionic_path_t2 = {
	desc = {

			}

	start_value = 0
	progress_direction = monodirectional

	on_start = {
		set_situation_locked = yes
	}

	on_fail = {

		owner = {

				type = situation_tec_biopsionic_path_t2

				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = new_situation
				}
			}

			set_situation_locked = no
		}

		}
	}

				}

	situation_tec_test = {
		desc = {
			text = situation_tec_test_desc
			trigger = {
				hidden_trigger = {
					always = yes
				}
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_cybernetics
		category = positive
		complete_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_green
		complete_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_unknown
		fail_icon_frame = GFX_situation_outcome_frame_red
		fail_icon = GFX_situation_outcome_negative
		start_value = 0
		progress_direction = monodirectional

		on_start = {
			set_situation_locked = no
		}

		on_fail = {

		}

		on_monthly = {
			random_events = {
				# Nothing
				200 = 0
			}
		}
		
		on_progress_complete = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = tec_situation_test
					}
				}
				owner = {
					set_country_flag = tec_situation_test			
				}
				owner = {
					start_situation = {
						type = situation_tec_test
						target = capital_scope
						effect = {
							save_event_target_as = new_situation
						}
					}
					event_target:new_situation = {
						set_situation_locked = no
						set_situation_approach = situation_approach_tec_test_neutral
					}
				}
			}
		}

		stages = {
			situation_tec_test_stage_1 = { #25% - After unlocks approaches
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_1
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_orange
				end = 25
			}

			situation_tec_test_stage_2 = { #50%
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_2
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_tec_yellow
				end = 50
				on_first_enter = {
					hidden_effect = {
						set_situation_flag = situation_tec_psionic_path_t2_approachs
					}
				}
			}

			situation_tec_test_stage_3 = { #75%
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_3
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_green
				end = 75
			}

			situation_tec_test_stage_4 = { #100%
				icon = GFX_situation_stage_4
				icon_background = GFX_situation_stage_frame_blue
				end = 100
				on_first_enter = {
					hidden_effect = {
						
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Approaches
		approach = { # Slow but good
			name = situation_approach_tec_test_slow
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_gear
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_green
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_test_slow
				#custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_test_slow_tooltip
			}
			resources = {
				category = situations
				upkeep = {
					society_research = 10
				}
			}
		}

		approach = { # Basic
			name = situation_approach_tec_test_neutral
			icon = GFX_situation_approach_research
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_yellow
			on_select = {
				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_test_neutral
				#custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_test_neutral_tooltip
			}

				}
			}
		}

			icon = GFX_situation_approach_tec_genecrank
			icon_background = GFX_situation_approach_bg_red

				custom_tooltip = situation_approach_tec_test_fast
